country_event = { 
	id = flavor_hyw.01
	title = "flavor_hyw.01.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.01.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.VICTORY2"
		france_superregion = { 
			limit = { 
				is_city = yes
				owned_by = ENG
				NOT = { 
					province_id = 63
				}
			}
			add_core = ROOT
		}
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:won conflict with Plantagenet, got cores on france_superregion:flavor_hyw.01"
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = flavor_hyw.06
	title = "flavor_hyw.06.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.06.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		ouest_france_region = { 
			limit = { 
				owned_by = ROOT
			}
			add_core = ROOT
		}
		ouest_france_region = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim = ROOT
		}
		languedoc_region = { 
			limit = { 
				owned_by = ROOT
			}
			add_core = ROOT
		}
		languedoc_region = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.VICTORY2"
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:won conflict with Valois, got cores on ouest_france_region and languedoc_region:flavor_hyw.06"
	}
}
country_event = { 
	id = flavor_hyw.07
	title = "flavor_hyw.06.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.07.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.VICTORY2"
		reverse_add_aggressive_expansion = { 
			who = ENG
			value = 50
			apply_calc = yes
		}
		FRA = { 
			every_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					superregion = france_superregion
					controlled_by = FRA
				}
				cede_province = ROOT
			}
			remove_government_reform = salic_law_reform
			add_government_reform = Pol_Succession1
		}
		FRA = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = flavor_hyw.91
				days = 1
			}
		}
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:got crowned as king of France:flavor_hyw.07"
	}
}
country_event = { 
	id = flavor_hyw.08
	title = "flavor_hyw.06.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.08.d"

			}
		}
		add_prestige = 25
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:got crowned as king of France and created Permanent PU:flavor_hyw.08"
	}
}
country_event = { 
	id = flavor_hyw.11
	title = "flavor_hyw.11.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.11.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	major = yes
	trigger = { 
		has_global_flag = hundred_years_war
		tag = ENG
		NOT = { 
			dynasty = "Plantagenet"
			dynasty = "Lancaster"
			dynasty = "York"
		}
		OR = { 
			has_regency = no
			has_consort_regency = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6
	}
	immediate = { 
		clr_global_flag = hundred_years_war
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]::flag hundred_years_war was cleared:flavor_hyw.11"
		set_global_flag = hundred_years_war_FRA_win
		FRA = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = flavor_hyw.01
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.FIGHT"
		random_list = { 
			30 = { }
			40 = { 
				hidden_effect = { 
					change_variable = { 
						which = ahf
						value = -600
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							AND = { 
								check_variable = { 
									which = ahf
									value = 1200
								}
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								stability = 3
							}
							set_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 1200
							}
						}
						else = { 
							subtract_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 1200
							}
							add_stability = 1
						}
					}
					else_if = { 
						limit = { 
							NOT = { 
								AND = { 
									check_variable = { 
										which = ahf
										value = 0
									}
								}
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								NOT = { 
									stability = -2
								}
							}
							set_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 0
							}
						}
						else = { 
							change_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 1200
							}
							add_stability = -1
						}
					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						which = ahf
					}
					divide_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						value = 12
					}
					multiply_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						value = 0.1
					}
					multiply_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						value = 10
					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = lsc
						value = 100
					}
					subtract_variable = { 
						which = lsc
						which = ahd
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = POP_StabSubtract50
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						is_emperor_of_china = yes
					}
					add_mandate = -2.5
				}
			}
			30 = { 
				hidden_effect = { 
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							NOT = { 
								stability = -2
							}
						}
						set_variable = { 
							which = ahf
							value = 0
						}
					}
					else = { 
						add_stability = -1
					}
				}
				tooltip = { 
					add_stability = -1
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						is_emperor_of_china = yes
					}
					add_mandate = -5
				}
			}
		}
		capital_scope = { 
			pretender_rebels = 2
		}
		custom_tooltip = hyw_ending_explanation
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:Plantagenet dynasty died out, but HYW continued:flavor_hyw.11"
	}
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.YIELD"
		every_province = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					owned_by = FRA
					owner = { 
						is_subject_of = FRA
					}
				}
				superregion = france_superregion
				is_core = ROOT
			}
			remove_core = ROOT
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { 
						accepted_culture = PREV
					}
				}
				ROOT = { 
					remove_accepted_culture = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = hyw_ending_explanation
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:Plantagenet dynasty died out, HYW ended:flavor_hyw.11"
	}
}
country_event = { 
	id = flavor_hyw.12
	title = "flavor_hyw.11.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.12.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	major = yes
	trigger = { 
		tag = FRA
		NOT = { 
			dynasty = "de Valois"
		}
		has_global_flag = hundred_years_war
		OR = { 
			has_regency = no
			has_consort_regency = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 6
	}
	immediate = { 
		clr_global_flag = hundred_years_war

		set_global_flag = hundred_years_war_ENG_win
		ENG = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = flavor_hyw.06
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.FIGHT"
		random_list = { 
			30 = { }
			40 = { 
				hidden_effect = { 
					change_variable = { 
						which = ahf
						value = -600
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							AND = { 
								check_variable = { 
									which = ahf
									value = 1200
								}
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								stability = 3
							}
							set_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 1200
							}
						}
						else = { 
							subtract_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 1200
							}
							add_stability = 1
						}
					}
					else_if = { 
						limit = { 
							NOT = { 
								AND = { 
									check_variable = { 
										which = ahf
										value = 0
									}
								}
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								NOT = { 
									stability = -2
								}
							}
							set_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 0
							}
						}
						else = { 
							change_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 1200
							}
							add_stability = -1
						}
					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						which = ahf
					}
					divide_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						value = 12
					}
					multiply_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						value = 0.1
					}
					multiply_variable = { 
						which = ahd
						value = 10
					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = lsc
						value = 100
					}
					subtract_variable = { 
						which = lsc
						which = ahd
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = POP_StabSubtract50
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						is_emperor_of_china = yes
					}
					add_mandate = -2.5
				}
			}
			30 = { 
				hidden_effect = { 
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							NOT = { 
								stability = -2
							}
						}
						set_variable = { 
							which = ahf
							value = 0
						}
					}
					else = { 
						add_stability = -1
					}
				}
				tooltip = { 
					add_stability = -1
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						is_emperor_of_china = yes
					}
					add_mandate = -5
				}
			}
		}
		capital_scope = { 
			pretender_rebels = 2
		}
		custom_tooltip = hyw_ending_explanation
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:de Valois dynasty died out, but HYW continued:flavor_hyw.12"
	}
	option = { 
		name = "OPT.YIELD"
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:de Valois dynasty died out, HYW ended:flavor_hyw.12"
		ouest_france_region = { 
			limit = { 
				is_city = yes
				owned_by = ENG
				is_core = ROOT
			}
			remove_core = ROOT
		}
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:lost cores in ouest_france_region:flavor_hyw.12"
		languedoc_region = { 
			limit = { 
				is_city = yes
				owned_by = ENG
				is_core = ROOT
			}

		}
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:lost cores in languedoc_region:flavor_hyw.12"
		custom_tooltip = hyw_ending_explanation
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = flavor_hyw.18
	title = "flavor_hyw.18.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.18.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	major = yes
	trigger = { 
		tag = ENG
		NOT = { 
			war_with = FRA
		}
		NOT = { 
			truce_with = FRA
		}
		FRA = { 
			exists = yes
			check_variable = { 
				which = "Demesne_in_France"
				value = 10
			}
		}
		check_variable = { 
			which = "Demesne_in_France"
			value = 3
		}
		NOT = { 
			check_variable = { 
				which = "Demesne_in_France"
				value = 5
			}
		}
		stability = 0
		NOT = { 
			war_exhaustion = 5
		}
		is_at_war = no
		has_global_flag = hundred_years_war
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		years = 5
	}
	option = { 
		name = "flavor_hyw.18.a"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 75
			modifier = { 
				is_year = 1450
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_prestige = 10
		declare_war_with_cb = { 
			who = FRA
			casus_belli = cb_hyw_treaty
		}
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:declared war againts France for a French throne:flavor_hyw.18"
	}
	option = { 
		name = "flavor_hyw.18.b"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 25
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					is_year = 1400
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_prestige = -10
		random_owned_province = { 
			pretender_rebels = 2
		}
		clr_global_flag = hundred_years_war
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]::flag hundred_years_war was cleared:flavor_hyw.18"
		set_global_flag = hundred_years_war_FRA_win
		custom_tooltip = hyw_ending_explanation
		log = "FE-TempHYW:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:yielded claims for a French throne:flavor_hyw.18"
	}
}

	id = flavor_hyw.19
	title = "flavor_hyw.19.t"
	desc = "flavor_hyw.19.d"

	trigger = { 
		tag = FRA
		ENG = { 
			exists = yes

				value = 5
			}
		}
		NOT = {

		}
		NOT = { 
			truce_with = ENG
		}
		stability = 0
		NOT = { 
			war_exhaustion = 5
		}
		is_at_war = no
		has_global_flag = hundred_years_war
		AND = { 
			check_variable = { 
				which = ohq
				value = ENG
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		years = 5
	}
	option = { 
		name = "flavor_hyw.19.a"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 75
			modifier = { 
				is_year = 1450
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_prestige = 10
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				180 = { 
					owned_by = GUY
					controlled_by = GUY
